\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Double-\/ended queue of bounded size, allowing lock-\/free atomic access. \doxylink{class____gnu__parallel_1_1___restricted_bounded_concurrent_queue_a2ac4fcc26b5a8e8d3db9993ca3b6f777}{push\+\_\+front()} and \doxylink{class____gnu__parallel_1_1___restricted_bounded_concurrent_queue_a4b760899cefaccb86586c447b12c4cc3}{pop\+\_\+front()} must not be called concurrently to each other, while \doxylink{class____gnu__parallel_1_1___restricted_bounded_concurrent_queue_aff5854a49d63fcd08aae08eb282361e7}{pop\+\_\+back()} can be called concurrently at all times. {\ttfamily empty()}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_a3d1e3edfcf61ca2d831883e1afbad89e}{size()}}, and {\ttfamily top()} are intentionally not provided. Calling them would not make sense in a concurrent setting. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Splits several sorted sequences at a certain global \+\_\+\+\_\+rank, resulting in a splitting point for each sequence. The sequences are passed via a sequence of random-\/access iterator pairs, none of the sequences may be empty. If there are several equal elements across the split, the ones on the \+\_\+\+\_\+left side will be chosen from sequences with smaller number. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

Compare-\/and-\/swap. 

Compare {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+\_\+\+\_\+ptr} and {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+comparand}. If equal, let {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+\_\+\+\_\+ptr=\+\_\+\+\_\+replacement} and return {\ttfamily true}, return {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

function to split a sequence into parts of almost equal size. 

The resulting sequence \+\_\+\+\_\+s of length \+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads+1 contains the splitting positions when splitting the range \mbox{[}0,\+\_\+\+\_\+n) into parts of almost equal size (plus minus 1). The first entry is 0, the last one n. There may result empty parts.

\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads} & Number of parts \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+s} & Splitters \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
End of \+\_\+\+\_\+splitter sequence, i.\+e. {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+s+\+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+threads+1} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Work stealing algorithm for random access iterators. 

Uses \doxylink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{O(1)} additional memory. Synchronization at job lists is done with atomic operations.

\hline

Merge routine being able to merge only the {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+max\+\_\+length} smallest elements. 

The {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+begin} iterators are advanced accordingly, they might not reach {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+end}, in contrast to the usual variant. Static switch on whether to use the conditional-\/move variant.

Merge routine being able to merge only the {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+max\+\_\+length} smallest elements. 

The {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+begin} iterators are advanced accordingly, they might not reach {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+end}, in contrast to the usual variant. Specially designed code should allow the compiler to generate conditional moves instead of branches.

The {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+begin} iterators are advanced accordingly, they might not reach {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+end}, in contrast to the usual variant. The functionality is projected onto parallel\+\_\+multiway\+\_\+merge.

Splits a sequence given by input iterators into parts of almost equal size. 

The function needs only one pass over the sequence. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+begin} & Begin iterator of input sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+end} & End iterator of input sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+starts} & Start iterators for the resulting parts, dimension {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+parts+1}. For convenience, {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+starts} {\ttfamily }\mbox{[}\+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+parts\mbox{]} contains the end iterator of the sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+lengths} & Length of the resulting parts. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+num\+\_\+parts} & Number of parts to split the sequence into. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+f} & Functor to be applied to each element by traversing \+\_\+\+\_\+it \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+oversampling} & Oversampling factor. If 0, then the partitions will differ in at most $\sqrt{\mathrm{end} - \mathrm{begin}}$ elements. Otherwise, the ratio between the longest and the shortest part is bounded by $1/(\mathrm{oversampling} \cdot \mathrm{num\_parts})$ \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Length of the whole sequence. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_e_g_l_2eglext_8h_a0f7193911e632cd84da4082d5c628fe3}{void}} \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+parallel\+::multiseq\+\_\+partition (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Ran\+Seqs}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+begin\+\_\+seqs,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Ran\+Seqs}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+end\+\_\+seqs,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Rank\+Type}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+rank,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Rank\+Iterator}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+begin\+\_\+offsets,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Compare}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+comp = {\ttfamily std\+:\+:less$<$~\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}}~std\+:\+:iterator\+\_\+traits$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}}~std\+:\+:iterator\+\_\+traits$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Ran\+Seqs}}$>$\+:\+:value\+\_\+type\+:\+:~\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{first\+\_\+type}}$>$\+:\+:value\+\_\+type$>$()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Splits several sorted sequences at a certain global \+\_\+\+\_\+rank, resulting in a splitting point for each sequence. The sequences are passed via a sequence of random-\/access iterator pairs, none of the sequences may be empty. If there are several equal elements across the split, the ones on the \+\_\+\+\_\+left side will be chosen from sequences with smaller number. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+begin\+\_\+seqs} & Begin of the sequence of iterator pairs. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+end\+\_\+seqs} & End of the sequence of iterator pairs. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+rank} & The global rank to partition at. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+begin\+\_\+offsets} & A random-\/access \+\_\+\+\_\+sequence \+\_\+\+\_\+begin where the \+\_\+\+\_\+result will be stored in. Each element of the sequence is an iterator that points to the first element on the greater part of the respective \+\_\+\+\_\+sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+comp} & The ordering functor, defaults to std\+::less$<$\+\_\+\+Tp$>$. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Difference\+Tp}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Compare}} $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}} \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+parallel\+::multiway\+\_\+merge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+target,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Difference\+Tp}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Compare}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+comp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct____gnu__parallel_1_1sequential__tag}{\+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+parallel\+::sequential\+\_\+tag}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Multiway Merge Frontend. 

Merge the sequences specified by seqs\+\_\+begin and \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end into \+\_\+\+\_\+target. \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin and \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end must point to a sequence of pairs. These pairs must contain an iterator to the beginning of a sequence in their first entry and an iterator the \+\_\+\+M\+\_\+end of the same sequence in their second entry.

Ties are broken arbitrarily. See stable\+\_\+multiway\+\_\+merge for a variant that breaks ties by sequence number but is slower.

The first entries of the pairs (i.\+e. the begin iterators) will be moved forward.

The output sequence has to provide enough space for all elements that are written to it.

This function will merge the input sequences\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item not stable
\item parallel, depending on the input size and Settings
\item using sampling for splitting
\item not using sentinels
\end{DoxyItemize}

Example\+:


\begin{DoxyPre}
  int sequences[10][10];
  for (int \_\_i = 0; \_\_i < 10; ++\_\_i)
    for (int \_\_j = 0; \_\_i < 10; ++\_\_j)
      sequences[\_\_i][\_\_j] = \_\_j;

  int \_\_out[33];
  std::vector<std::pair<int*> > seqs;
  for (int \_\_i = 0; \_\_i < 10; ++\_\_i)
    \{ seqs.push(std::make\_pair<int*>(sequences[\_\_i],
                                     sequences[\_\_i] + 10)) \}

  multiway\_merge(seqs.begin(), seqs.end(), \_\_target, std::less<int>(), 33);
\end{DoxyPre}


\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{namespace____gnu__parallel_a27f5da3fdd4d5f56eecd6a078ec7bae2}{stable\+\_\+multiway\+\_\+merge}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
All input sequences must be sorted. 

Target must provide enough space to merge out length elements or the number of elements in all sequences, whichever is smaller.
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
\mbox{[}\+\_\+\+\_\+target, return \+\_\+\+\_\+value) contains merged \+\_\+\+\_\+elements from the input sequences. 

return \+\_\+\+\_\+value -\/ \+\_\+\+\_\+target = min(\+\_\+\+\_\+length, number of elements in all    sequences).
\end{DoxyPostcond}

Highly efficient 3-\/way merging procedure. 

Merging is done with the algorithm implementation described by Peter Sanders. Basically, the idea is to minimize the number of necessary comparison after merging an element. The implementation trick that makes this fast is that the order of the sequences is stored in the instruction pointer (translated into labels in C++).

This works well for merging up to 4 sequences.

Note that making the merging stable does {\itshape not} come at a performance hit.

Whether the merging is done guarded or unguarded is selected by the used iterator class.

{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin} & Begin iterator of iterator pair input sequence. \\

\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+target} & Begin iterator of output sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+comp} & Comparator. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+length} & Maximum length to merge, less equal than the total number of elements available.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
End iterator of output sequence. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Highly efficient 4-\/way merging procedure. 

Merging is done with the algorithm implementation described by Peter Sanders. Basically, the idea is to minimize the number of necessary comparison after merging an element. The implementation trick that makes this fast is that the order of the sequences is stored in the instruction pointer (translated into goto labels in C++).

This works well for merging up to 4 sequences.

Note that making the merging stable does {\itshape not} come at a performance hit.

Whether the merging is done guarded or unguarded is selected by the used iterator class.

Multi-\/way merging procedure for a high branching factor, guarded case. 

This merging variant uses a Loser\+Tree class as selected by {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+LT}.

Stability is selected through the used Loser\+Tree class {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+LT}.

At least one non-\/empty sequence is required.

\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+comp} & Comparator. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+length} & Maximum length to merge, less equal than the total number of elements available.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
End iterator of output sequence. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Difference\+Tp}} , \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{typename}} \mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Compare}} $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}} \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+parallel\+::multiway\+\_\+merge\+\_\+sentinels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Pair\+Iterator}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+RAIter\+Out}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+target,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Difference\+Tp}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+length,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_g_l_e_s2_2gl2ext_8h_ae60229696c2ec17c9e00af4899bf738e}{\+\_\+\+Compare}}}]{\+\_\+\+\_\+comp,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct____gnu__parallel_1_1sequential__tag}{\+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+parallel\+::sequential\+\_\+tag}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Multiway Merge Frontend. 

Merge the sequences specified by seqs\+\_\+begin and \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end into \+\_\+\+\_\+target. \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin and \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end must point to a sequence of pairs. These pairs must contain an iterator to the beginning of a sequence in their first entry and an iterator the \+\_\+\+M\+\_\+end of the same sequence in their second entry.

Ties are broken arbitrarily. See stable\+\_\+multiway\+\_\+merge for a variant that breaks ties by sequence number but is slower.

The first entries of the pairs (i.\+e. the begin iterators) will be moved forward accordingly.

The output sequence has to provide enough space for all elements that are written to it.

This function will merge the input sequences\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item not stable
\item parallel, depending on the input size and Settings
\item using sampling for splitting
\item using sentinels
\end{DoxyItemize}

You have to take care that the element the \+\_\+\+M\+\_\+end iterator points to is readable and contains a value that is greater than any other non-\/sentinel value in all sequences.

Example\+:


\begin{DoxyPre}
  int sequences[10][11];
  for (int \_\_i = 0; \_\_i < 10; ++\_\_i)
    for (int \_\_j = 0; \_\_i < 11; ++\_\_j)
      sequences[\_\_i][\_\_j] = \_\_j; // \_\_last one is sentinel!

  int \_\_out[33];
  std::vector<std::pair<int*> > seqs;
  for (int \_\_i = 0; \_\_i < 10; ++\_\_i)
    \{ seqs.push(std::make\_pair<int*>(sequences[\_\_i],
                                     sequences[\_\_i] + 10)) \}

  multiway\_merge(seqs.begin(), seqs.end(), \_\_target, std::less<int>(), 33);
\end{DoxyPre}


\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
All input sequences must be sorted. 

Target must provide enough space to merge out length elements or the number of elements in all sequences, whichever is smaller. 

For each {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+i}, {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin}\mbox{[}\+\_\+\+\_\+i\mbox{]}.second must be the end marker of the sequence, but also reference the one more \+\_\+\+\_\+sentinel element.
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxyPostcond}{Postcondition}
\mbox{[}\+\_\+\+\_\+target, return \+\_\+\+\_\+value) contains merged \+\_\+\+\_\+elements from the input sequences. 

return \+\_\+\+\_\+value -\/ \+\_\+\+\_\+target = min(\+\_\+\+\_\+length, number of elements in all    sequences).
\end{DoxyPostcond}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Parallel multi-\/way merge routine. 

The \+\_\+\+GLIBCXX\+\_\+\+PARALLEL\+\_\+\+DECISION is based on the branching factor and runtime settings.

Must not be called if the number of sequences is 1.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em \+\_\+\+Splitter} & functor to split input (either \+\_\+\+\_\+exact or sampling based) \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+stable} & Stable merging incurs a performance penalty. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+sentinel} & Ignored.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+begin} & Begin iterator of iterator pair input sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+seqs\+\_\+end} & End iterator of iterator pair input sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+target} & Begin iterator of output sequence. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+comp} & Comparator. \\
\hline
{\em \+\_\+\+\_\+length} & Maximum length to merge, possibly larger than the number of elements available. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
End iterator of output sequence. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
